    <td style="text-align: center"><span style="font-size: 10pt">The <span id="xdx_907_edei--SecurityExchangeName_c20240313__20240313__us-gaap--StatementClassOfStockAxis__custom--WarrantsToPurchaseSharesOfCommonStockMember_zaCXOZRa4nHe"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="From2024-03-132024-03-13_custom_WarrantsToPurchaseSharesOfCommonStockMember" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" name="dei:SecurityExchangeName" id="ixv-360">NASDAQ</ix:nonNumeric></span>&#160;Stock Market LLC</span></td></tr>
  </table>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Indicate by check mark
whether the registrant is an emerging growth company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter)&#160;or
Rule 12b-2 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b-2 of this chapter).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Emerging growth
company <span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><span id="xdx_908_edei--EntityEmergingGrowthCompany_c20240313__20240313_zou9Lz7hmPo8"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="AsOf2024-03-13" format="ixt:booleanfalse" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany" id="ixv-361">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">If an emerging
growth company, indicate by check mark if the registrant has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with
any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant to Section 13(a)&#160;of the Exchange Act. <span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&#9744;</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><b>Item 8.01 Other Events.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">As previously disclosed, on
September 7, 2023, 180 Life Sciences Corp. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Company</span>&#8221;) received a notification letter from The Nasdaq Stock Market
LLC (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Nasdaq</span>&#8221;) indicating that the Company&#8217;s common stock failed to maintain a minimum bid price of $1.00 over
the previous 30 consecutive business days as required by Nasdaq Listing Rule 5550(a)(2).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On March 13, 2024, the Company
received a letter from Nasdaq notifying the Company that it has regained full compliance with the minimum bid price for continued listing
on Nasdaq, pursuant to Nasdaq Listing Rule&#160;5550(a)(2)(the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Minimum Bid Price Requirement</span>&#8221;), because Nasdaq has
determined that for 10 consecutive business days, the closing bid price of the Company&#8217;s common stock was at or above $1.00 per
share.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">Accordingly, the Company has
regained compliance with the Minimum Bid Price Requirement and the matter is now closed.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">Notwithstanding the above,
and as discussed in the Current Reports on Form 8-K filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on November 16, 2023 and January
16, 2024, the Company remains out of compliance with the minimum stockholders&#8217; equity requirement for continued listing on the Nasdaq
Capital Market. Nasdaq Listing Rule 5550(b)(1) (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Rule</span>&#8221;), which requires companies listed on the Nasdaq Capital
Market to maintain stockholders&#8217; equity of at least $2,500,000. In the Company&#8217;s Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the quarter
ended September 30, 2023, the Company reported a stockholders&#8217; deficit of ($149,327), which is below the minimum stockholders&#8217;
equity required for continued listing pursuant to the Rule. Additionally, the Company does not meet the alternative Nasdaq continued listing
standards under Nasdaq Listing Rules. The Company is currently evaluating various courses of action to regain compliance and is hopeful
that it can regain compliance with Nasdaq&#8217;s minimum stockholders&#8217; equity standard within the compliance period approved by
Nasdaq; however, there can be no assurance that the Company will be able to complete the transactions contemplated in the compliance plan,
which the Company expects will allow it to regain compliance with the Rule, or that such transactions will result in the Company regaining
compliance with the Rule, within the compliance period granted by Nasdaq, if at all.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in">On March 14, 2024, the Company
filed a press release disclosing the fact that it has regained compliance with the Minimum Bid Price Requirement. A copy of the press
release is included herewith as&#160;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Exhibit 99.1</span>&#160;and the information in the press
release is incorporated by reference into this <span style="text-decoration: underline">Item 8.01</span>.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; background-color: white"><b></b></p>

<DESCRIPTION>PRESS RELEASE, DATED MARCH 14, 2024
<TEXT>
<HTML>
<HEAD>
     <TITLE></TITLE>
</HEAD>
<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>180 Life Sciences Regains Full Compliance with
Nasdaq</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Minimum Bid Price Requirement</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: #FEFEFE"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>PALO ALTO, Calif., March 14, 2024&nbsp;</B>--
180 Life Sciences Corp. (NASDAQ: ATNF) (&ldquo;180 Life Sciences&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;), today announced that the Company
received a letter on March 13, 2024 from The Nasdaq Stock Market LLC (&ldquo;Nasdaq&rdquo;) indicating that the Company has regained full
compliance with the minimum bid price for continued listing on the Nasdaq pursuant to Nasdaq Listing Rule&nbsp;5550(a)(2) (&ldquo;Minimum
Bid Price Requirement&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">As indicated in the letter, Nasdaq determined
that for 10 consecutive business days, the closing bid price of the Company&rsquo;s common stock was at or above $1.00 per share. Accordingly,
the Company has regained compliance with the Minimum Bid Price Requirement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>About 180 Life Sciences Corp.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">180 Life Sciences Corp. is a clinical stage biotechnology
company focused on the development of therapeutics for unmet medical needs in chronic pain, inflammation and fibrosis by employing innovative
research, and, where appropriate, combination therapy. The Company&rsquo;s current primary focus is a novel program to treat several inflammatory
disorders using anti-TNF (tumor necrosis factor).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>Investors:</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Jason Assad</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Director of IR</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">180 Life Sciences Corp</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Jason@180lifesciences.com</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>
